Public Telegram

The Huaiyin County Flood Relief Association Appeals to Shanghai Shenbao for Urgent Aid: Huaiyin is a poor and barren land, and has suffered from disasters and famines in recent years. Moreover, last year it suffered a terrible bandit robbery, and the people's strength has been exhausted. This spring, the wheat suffered from frost and drought, and the harvest was meager. Since summer, the weather has been timely, and the rice seedlings have grown luxuriantly. It was hoped that there would be a good autumn harvest and the people's difficulties would be slightly alleviated. How could it have been that since July, continuous rain has led to flooding of Hong Lake, which has been increasing daily and has not stopped. Initially, various sections of the lake beach were successively submerged. Now it has even reached the Taihuang Dam. Areas 2, 6, and 7 are all under water. Boats travel above the houses in Shunheji. Towns such as Zhangjiaxu, Zhaojiaji, Xiaoqiao Town, Tanghe, Jiubao, Taozha, Chenji, Xiaowangji, Wuji, and Zhengchang are all three to five feet deep in water. The south of the Grand Canal in Area 1 has suffered repeated flooding from the breaches in Huai'an 5, 6, 7, 8, Wanban, Yangjiamiao, Chahe, and Wanjii. Houses and sorghum have mostly collapsed into the water. Six hundred thousand acres of good farmland have all been turned into habitats for fish. Cooking smoke has ceased, and there is no sound of chickens and dogs. Only treetops and rooftops can be seen swaying amidst the frightened waves. Hundreds of thousands of victims are living in the open on the Taihuang and Hong Lake Dams. Such a tragic situation is unprecedented in a hundred years. Recently, a flood relief committee has been organized by local communities to first raise funds and select the most needy for relief. However, the disaster area is too wide and there are too many victims. A drop in the bucket is of no help. For this reason, we exhaustively report the disaster situation and appeal to all great philanthropists to send personnel to rush to provide urgent aid so that we can barely survive and avoid the extreme urgency of waiting for death. The Huaiyin Flood Relief Committee, He Zhoucheng, Li Yushu, Wang Shuxiang, Zhou Yuankai, Ni Jiafu, Han Zhao, Qian Danquan, Zhang Lupin, Fu Bingqi, etc. gratefully kowtow.

Important News

Russian Citizens Arbitrarily Move Boundary Markers on the Northeast Border

Encroaching on Our Country's Territory and Expelling Our Country's Farmers

Harbin Correspondence, Suifenhe News, The Fifth General Department of the Special Police learned some time ago that the Soviet Union had privately moved the northern border stone marker in the territory of Dongning County. It specially sent a commissioner to secretly investigate. According to the report, it is said that in the area north of Dongning County, Dongdachuan Wengan Dingzi, the Soviet Union privately moved the Japanese character boundary marker of the national border westward, encroaching on our territory by two or three li or four or five li. The farmers who had been cultivating in that area for many years were told by several Russian cavalrymen that they were occupying and cultivating their land, and they forcibly expelled the farmers with force. More than fifty farmers argued with them, but the Russian soldiers did not listen, arrested several farmers, and seized horses and oxen, etc., and detained them in the Russian territory for many days. They forced each farmer to sign a statement that they would no longer cultivate the land before releasing them. However, the farmer Zhang Zenggui refused to sign because his fields, houses, and tombs were all in that area, and he has been detained by the Russians to this day. Also, in Taipinggou, 20 li north of Dongning City and Dachuan, on a hillside about 2.5 li west of the old national border, several new wooden posts were discovered that had been buried by the Soviets. Russian border characters and Arabic numeral "1" were written on them, and they were covered with loose soil, intending to pretend that they had been buried for a long time. The Dongning County government discovered this, sent personnel to pull them out, and burned them. However, in various places south of Dongning County, the border markers have recently been secretly removed by the Russians and thrown into the valleys. The national border markers have been buried, and it is no longer possible to distinguish between the Russian and Chinese areas. The Dongning County Magistrate has already telegraphed the Provincial Government for instructions. On the one hand, a protest has been lodged with the Russian officials, demanding the rescue and release of the farmers (19th).

The Yalu River Water Level Rises, but the Crisis Has Passed

Severe Flooding in Western Korea

Andong Correspondence, From the beginning of this month to the 20th, continuous rain continued for two weeks. The Yalu River, both upstream and downstream, rose in water level, with turbulent waves and overflowing floods. Residents and merchants in this port were worried that the flood disaster of the 12th year of the Republic of China would strike again and were all wary. On the 16th, from 10:00 AM to 12:00 PM, the tide was at its highest, and the river rose to its most dangerous level. According to measurements taken by personnel sent by the county government, the average water level on that morning was one zhang, seven or eight chi. Low-lying areas in the city had become a swamp. The Jiang'an Bridge area outside the city was flooded with water about four chi deep or more on the morning of the 15th, and nearby merchants and residents were cut off from transportation. At the same time, six or seven sailboats were there to carry merchants and residents to the city for refuge. The Japanese and Korean residents of the nearby Jiang'an Tong area were moved to shelters under the command of the Japanese police to avoid disaster. During the three days of the 14th, 15th and 16th, when the water level rose sharply, the Andong County Office dispatched Yin Section Chief to supervise section chiefs and staff to patrol the river embankment in groups and dispatched special personnel to defend each sluice gate. The Yalu River Logging Company reported by telegram from the upstream branch offices during the three days of the 14th, 15th and 16th that on the 14th, the Maishitai water level rose one zhang, the Waichagou water level rose seven chi, and the Baicaidi water level rose one zhang and two chi. On the 15th, the Baicaidi water level continued to rise three chi, and the Waichagou water level continued to rise five chi. On the 16th, the Waichagou water level rose another five chi, and the Baicaidi water level rose another seven chi. The Maishitai water level continued to rise five chi. After 2:00 PM on the 16th, reports of receding water levels began to arrive one after another. The water level of the Yalu River upstream and downstream has turned from danger to safety.

As for the left bank of the Yalu River in western Korea, within Ping'an Province, rivers that flow directly into the Yalu River have been suffering. On the 14th, 15th and 16th, the water level rose sharply, exceeding the water level of the rivers within Yizhou County on the right bank of the Yalu River by about one zhang. In Jianchang County, the water level in the Jiayanli area rose about seven chi. In Bitong County, the Douman River rose nine chi. Long-distance automobiles traveling to and from the area were temporarily suspended starting on the 14th. Automobiles traveling from Weiyuan County to Chushan were also suspended starting on the 14th. The Anman Motor Road near Manpu Town was washed away in more than ten places on the 13th. Automobiles traveling in both directions were immediately suspended. In Cicheng County, the Cicheng River rose eight chi on the 15th. In Jiangjie County, the Tulu River rose nine chi. The bridge in Beigong Township was washed away in fourteen dong. According to a survey by the Ping'an Province Office, the losses in its jurisdiction during these three days are at least over 350,000. On the 15th, at the Jichuan Township ferry in Chushan County, two Korean youths were crossing the river and tragically drowned in the middle. On the 15th, rocks near Songdong Village in Jiangdong Township, Taishan County, suddenly collapsed, crushing a family of five, old and young, from the family of Korean Kim Kwang-chang. Director of the Incheon Customs, Tanaka Hidesaburo, returned on the afternoon of the 17th in a car with a certain geisha. The driver stepped on the gas, but failed to stop when he reached the river bank. With a crash, the car fell into the river. The driver was lucky enough to escape, but Customs Director Tanaka and the geisha were tragically drowned together. After days of rain, plague has been discovered in the western part of Korea, and many have died. The Ping'an Province Office has dispatched many government doctors to go in the rain to prevent the epidemic (21st).

After the Harbin Navigation Joint Bureau Concluded

丨Merchant ships organize transportation offices still unite丨

Profits of two million yuan in the first half of the year.

Harbin Correspondence. This spring, in order to promote unity in the Songhua River shipping industry, there was an organization to expand the Joint Navigation Bureau. However, due to conflicts of interest, it was opposed by merchant groups in 14 counties along the Songhua, Heihe, and Wusuli Rivers. After half a year of mutual criticism, the Political Committee ordered the expanded joint navigation to be temporarily concluded at the end of last month and reconsidered next year. Thus, the Joint General Bureau of Shipping, a cooperation between officials and merchants, concluded yesterday. According to Mr. Wang Shize, the manager of the Northeast Shipping Bureau, about the closure of the Joint Navigation and the current state of shipping, it is roughly as follows:

Closure of the Joint Bureau of Official and Merchant Navigation. After the official and merchant Joint Shipping Bureau was ordered to close, the general merchant shareholders believed that it would not be easy to close the accounts and procedures in the middle, and asked the Northeast Shipping Bureau to request the Northeast authorities to allow a grace period until the river was closed, but it was still rejected. Therefore, the merchants despaired and had to proceed with the closure. Considering the nature of the shipping industry, it is different from other industries. The ships set sail with different distances to be traveled, and it would not be easy to change the situation after a morning of closure. After many discussions among the shipping companies, it was decided that August 15 would be the standard date for closure. Before this date, all ships would return to their home ports and would only be allowed to set sail after the closure. From April 23, when the Joint Navigation was established, to August 1, when the ships returned to their ports, the total profit for the half year was 2 million yuan. According to the shares of the ships that joined, each share could earn 0.35 yuan. However, because 500,000 yuan in outstanding debts had not been recovered, the actual profit distribution was only 25%. By August 14, the closure of each ship was completed and they were free to set sail. However, the Joint Navigation still had many events and procedures that had not been cleared, so it was not completely closed. Four ships sailing to the Jilin area were stranded in Jilin due to shallow water and have not returned. They will be closed separately in the future. A small number of personnel are still working in the Joint Navigation, and their salaries are scheduled to be paid until the end of the month. If the work cannot be completed by the end of the month, a few more people will be retained to handle it. In addition, a sailboat has a one-year lease relationship with the Joint Navigation Bureau. Due to the termination of the contract midway, it demanded more rent and has not been resolved to this day.

The current trend of shipping. After the closure of the large joint navigation bureau, the official ships will still be managed by the Northeast Shipping Bureau without much problem. Commercial ships are relatively difficult because although the general shipowners secretly grumbled when they joined the Joint Navigation, they sincerely wished the Joint Navigation to continue so that they could save their efforts. The dissolution of the official and merchant Joint Shipping Bureau and the management of their own business at this time is quite

Page 10

inconvenient. Therefore, some are still conducting on a smaller scale, forming a group of commercial ships to maintain it until the river is closed. However, most of the shipowners with appeal are passive and unwilling to take responsibility. At present, only the former Deputy Manager of the Grand Joint Navigation Bureau, Fu Zhongchen, is the General Manager, and the Chairman of the Board is Song Wenlin. The organization is named the Commercial Shipping Office, and is internally divided into two sections, temporarily working in the Ship Industry Association. The first batch of united ships has set sail. Whether the union will be consolidated will depend on the success of this trip. When the Joint Navigation Bureau existed, all parties attacked it with all their might due to different interests. There are several things that are most regrettable after its cancellation. (1) Remote routes, such as Jilin and Xingkai Lake, will never have ship service. (2) It is inconvenient to transport refugees, with officials and merchants shirking responsibility, unlike the convenience when the Joint Navigation Bureau existed. (3) It is not as convenient as before to transport military supplies. There are many other inconveniences that are difficult to achieve without the power of the large joint navigation. Therefore, the cancellation of this shipping union is extremely regrettable in terms of promoting benefits and facilitating the people (21st).

Remarks by Han Fuju After Arriving in Beiping

Yan Xishan's Return Has No Significant Impact

Mr. Feng Will Eventually Have to Go Abroad

Han Immediately Visits Zhang Xueliang at the Hospital

Beiping Correspondence: Han Fuju, Chairman of Shandong Provincial Government, arrived in Beiping at 9:15 AM on the 22nd, having traveled north by special train from Jinan at 3:00 PM on the 21st due to the pacification of Hebei's military affairs and the need to discuss post-war arrangements in North China. Those accompanying Han included Jiang Bocheng, Song Shiyan, Chief of Staff Liu Shuxiang, Secretary-General Zhang Shaotang, Director of Industry Wang Fangting, Jinan Mayor Wen Chenglie, and many important military officials, along with two companies of guards. Han made the following remarks that day: "I have come to visit the Deputy Commander because he has recovered from his illness. The Deputy Commander also sent a telegram requesting my presence, so I came to Beiping to meet him, seek instructions on post-war arrangements in North China, and show domestic and foreign reactionaries that the more they provoke, the closer the generals in North China become. My stay in Beiping will depend on the Deputy Commander's wishes, but I plan to stay for a week and also visit Henan. I do not plan to go to Nanjing for the time being. As for post-war arrangements in North China, everything is under the guidance of the Commander-in-Chief and Deputy Commander. I am only doing my best within my responsibilities. Yan Xishan's return to Shanxi, outwardly expressing that he will not interfere in politics, is probably because it is too late. He cannot express his political views any longer. Last year, he had great power but was still unable to do anything. Now he only has tired soldiers from Shanxi Province and can do nothing. Moreover, the Shanxi army may not even be used by him. Therefore, Yan Xishan's return to Shanxi has no significant impact. As long as the generals in North China unite and sincerely support the Central Government, Yan will have to leave even if he doesn't want to. As for Mr. Feng Yuxiang, he will eventually have to go abroad because he has no army in Shanxi. Now, ten bandits could kidnap him. With Mr. Feng's character, he would never want to deal with bandits. The Shi Yousan's troops, who were incorporated, only number six to seven thousand. They are now being trained, and the organization will be reported to the Central Government for instructions. Because Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek has gone to Shanghai, I have not yet received a reply. Regarding provincial affairs, because I am from a military background, with limited talent and shallow knowledge, and unfamiliar with politics, I only know to work hard within my responsibilities. Therefore, instead of staying in the provincial capital, I often go to the countryside to take a look. Most people in Chinese society take the four words 'promotion and wealth' too seriously. Therefore, most officials now claim to be revolutionary, but their actions are exactly the opposite. The so-called revolution is nothing more than relieving the suffering of the people and seeking happiness for the people. Therefore, as long as officials do not act like merchants, always thinking of a short-term tenure, anything can be done. County magistrates, judges, and prosecutors are all so-called 'people-loving' officials, so their actions are especially important. Therefore, it is necessary to always see what they are doing. There are no bandits in Shandong Province, only scattered bandits on the border of Shandong and Henan, who gather at night and disperse in the morning, so there is no need to deploy troops to suppress them. Regarding the issue of opium prohibition, because of my personal nature, I don't know much about whether smoking is beneficial or harmful, but I see that smokers become weaker and weaker, so I oppose smoking. I have been with Mr. Feng Yuxiang for twenty years and have never left him. The reason for my previous departure was partly because Mr. Feng ordered the people to grow opium in Shaanxi and Gansu."

Wu Tiecheng, a member of the Central Committee, visited Mr. Han at around 11:00 AM on the 22nd and talked for about ten minutes. He received a phone call from the headquarters saying that Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang would come to Han's residence to visit. Han thought that since he came to visit Zhang, it would be inappropriate for Zhang to come first. Han then led Fan Pujiang and Jiang Bocheng to the hospital to visit Zhang and report everything, talking for more than ten minutes. Then he visited Yu Xuezhong and Wan Fulin, exchanged pleasantries briefly, and returned to the reception to rest. In the afternoon, Zhang arrived at Han's residence in plain clothes and a straw hat, carrying a cane, accompanied by Zhang Xueming. He said to Han that he had heard that Han had inspected the troops on the way, which was extremely tiring. Han said that he took the opportunity to pay his respects to the Deputy Commander and inspected the troops on the way, so it was not worthy of praise. They talked for more than twenty minutes, and Zhang returned to the hospital. In the afternoon, Han Fuju visited Shang Zhen, Bao Yulin, Zhou Dawen, Zhang Xueming, Pang Bingxun, and others, talking briefly and then leaving. (23rd)

Liu Zhenhua and Zhang Fang Pass Through Jinan: Liu Goes South, Zhang Goes North

Jinan Correspondence: Liu Zhenhua, Pacification Commissioner of the Henan-Shaanxi-Shanxi Border Area, passed through Jinan by special train from Tianjin to Nanjing today (23rd). He arrived at Jinan Station at 9:40 AM. Liu was wearing a gray woolen gown and looked a little older than the last time he passed through Shandong. He was accompanied by a few staff members and a platoon of guards. After Liu got off the train, he shook hands with those who welcomed him and was invited to the first-class waiting room by Li Shuchun, Sun Tongxuan, and others to rest. According to Liu, his troops are currently stationed in the Huaiqing area and may be transferred to Xinxiang in the future. Liu casually talked with Sun, Li, and others. Liu said that the Henan militia has more than 5,000 rifles in each county, and even small counties such as Pingdeng, Ziyou, and Bo'ai have 10,000 rifles, totaling no less than 300,000 rifles in the province. Regarding the recent situation in western Henan, he can tell Chairman Han after he returns to Jinan. Now, Wang Naiwen in Lushi County is still recruiting bandits on a large scale. In fact, the more bandits are recruited, the more there are. If they are not recruited, there will naturally be no bandits. Therefore, there is now a nursery rhyme in western Henan: "If you want to be an official, first sit on a pole; if you want to sit in a sedan chair, first sit in a temple," which means that becoming a bandit can lead to promotion at any time, and everyone takes pride in being a bandit, which really has a significant impact on society. Liu finally asked about the opium prohibition situation in Shandong. Li Shuchun told him that it has been very effective. Those who sell drugs often commit suicide by disembowelment or hanging themselves because if they sell Japanese goods or are caught, they cannot explain to the Japanese. However, there are still those who sell them. In Linqu, someone actually planted more than 70 acres of opium in the mountains. When the county magistrate found out, he uprooted them, and the people actually went to the province to sue, saying that the county magistrate was oppressing the people. Later, the Department of Civil Affairs sent a telegram to commend the county magistrate for his meritorious service, and the people dared not sue anymore. Liu also talked about the prevalence of drugs in Henan, with all kinds of strange things. Some people can get addicted by rubbing a piece of white paper with their hands. Those who sell drugs must be shot. At 10:15 AM, Liu boarded the train and headed south. The welcoming staff also left the station separately.

Zhang Fang, Commander of the 20th Route Army and Director of the Henan Department of Civil Affairs, arrived in Jinan from Nanjing on Train No. 202 at 6:00 PM today (23rd). According to Zhang, his mission is to discuss the issues of clearing the countryside in Shandong and Henan and disaster relief for the floods in Henan with Chairman Han. Now that Chairman Han has gone to Beiping, he will immediately go to Beiping. The bandits in Henan have not been completely eliminated. Most of his troops are stationed in the Nanyang area. Because they are stationed too scattered along the railway line, they can only defend the areas where they are stationed. It is a little inconvenient to gather troops to suppress the bandits. When the plan for clearing the countryside is completed in the future, the bandits will no longer be a problem. After Zhang got off the train, he stayed at the Jiaoji Hotel and will go to Beiping in the next few days. (23rd)

Shandong Yellow River Water Level Dropping, but Still Unpredictable Due to Wind and Rain

Zhang Lianjia Is Still Supervising the Emergency Rescue

Jinan Correspondence: Today, the upper, middle, and lower reaches of the Yellow River continue to report water level drops. The water level at Luokou is 8 feet 9 inches and 2 fen above sea level, which is 3 feet 8 inches lower than the highest water level this year. The situation is generally stable, but the northeast wind is strong today, and it rained again in the afternoon, so it is still difficult to predict what will happen in the future. Zhang Lianjia, Director of the River Affairs Bureau, is still inspecting the Dongzhuang and Lisheng Village areas in the upper reaches, supervising the emergency rescue. The water level reports from the following locations are recorded below: (1) Upper Reaches: Zhang Lufu and Wang Huaiyi reported that the water level at Lisheng Village was normal at 6:00 PM last night, with a water level of 17 zhang 3 chi 4 cun. The water level at Sunlou dropped 4 cun at 6:00 PM tonight, with a water level of 14 zhang 3 chi. (2) Middle Reaches: Zhang Yunpei and Wang Kuiqing reported from Guanzhuang that the water level dropped 3 cun at 6:00 PM tonight, with a water level of 10 zhang 6 chi. Zhou Ruyi and Liu Yuhe reported from the Ji River that the water level dropped 5 cun at 6:00 AM on the 23rd, with a water level of 9 zhang 5 chi 6 cun. They also reported that the water level dropped 4 cun at 6:00 PM on the 22nd, with a water level of 9 zhang 6 chi 1 cun. Qi Zongshou and Chen Kuiyuan reported from Xiaoluzhuang in Luokou that the water level dropped 5 cun at 6:00 AM on the 23rd, with a water level of 8 zhang 9 chi 3 cun. Bai Xizhi and Lu Chuanlun reported from Jiyang that the water level at the east gate was normal this morning, with a water level of 78 chi 3 cun. (3) Lower Reaches: Li Fuchang reported that the water level at Wangzaojia dropped 8 cun this morning and another 8 cun this evening, with a water level of 66 chi 3 cun. Yang Chenglin and Zhou Yumei reported that the water level at Tianwang Village dropped 5 cun from last night to this morning. Zheng Rongce and Li Baoren reported from Dama Village that the water level at Sunjia Village dropped 4 cun at 6:00 PM tonight, with a water level of 43 chi 4 cun. Wang Ziyuan, Director of the Public Security Bureau of Licheng County, reported today that the water level at Huojia Liuyu dropped a total of 3 chi 2 cun on the 21st, 22nd, and 23rd. (23rd)

The Investigation Report on the Xuzhou Flood Shows the Need for Urgent Relief

Xuzhou Correspondence: Since the Xuzhou area suffered a flood at the beginning of the month, a local flood relief association was formed to provide temporary relief and repeatedly telegraphed the provincial government to report the disaster, as well as sending representatives to the province to request relief. Recently, the provincial government sent Shen Tiecheng and Han Tongsheng to Xuzhou to investigate the disaster. According to the survey of the disaster area by the flood relief association, the main points are as follows: (1) Cause of the Disaster: Since the beginning of summer, there has been continuous rain, with particularly heavy rainfall from August 1st to 7th, with an average water depth of more than 2 chi in the whole county. In addition, the river channels in the whole county are silted up, the old Yellow River has flooded, and there are several breaches in Jizui Dam, Xiaobeimen, Hongfusi, Cangsheng Temple, and the Fire God Temple, which caused the disaster. (2) Loss Statistics: The total land area of Tongshan County is 3,600,000 mu, of which 2,160,000 mu were flooded, and 113,355 houses collapsed. (3) Affected Areas: The entire city and the 8th, 9th, 2nd, 3rd, 5th, 6th, and 7th districts were most severely affected. In addition, the 4th, 10th, 11th, and 12th districts were less affected. The average water level was more than 1 chi 5 cun. (4) Number of Affected People: The total population of the county is 986,536, of which 493,268 were affected, including 328,846 adults and 164,422 children. 148 people were injured and 105 people died. (5) Estimated Urgent Relief Funds: Each adult needs 1 jiao per day, and each child needs 5 fen per day. The amount of funds depends on the length of the relief period. It is estimated that 287,731 yuan will be needed within a week. (6) Relief Methods: One is to open more temporary ditches to divert water into the river and dredge the lower reaches of the old Yellow River to facilitate drainage. The other is to rebuild the old Yellow River embankment and the old ditches in the city, add sluice gates, deepen the old river, and dredge the river channels throughout the county to prevent future disasters. The relief association's survey and statistics are as follows. The county government has also sent personnel to various districts to investigate the disaster situation. The relief association started to provide shelter from the 10th and ended on the 16th. At present, the water in the city has receded, but the collapsed houses are waiting to be repaired, and there is a lack of labor and materials. Those who have no houses to live in are living with relatives and friends, and there is also a shortage of food and fuel. During the shelter period, only 1,455 disaster victims were accommodated. There are still many people outside the city who have not been reached. The provincial government has approved the allocation of 3,000 yuan, and Wang Jun has telegraphed Zheng to Xuzhou to instruct the garrison to provide assistance of 1,000 yuan. Liu Zhi has telegraphed Xuzhou from Bianjing to remit 1,000 yuan. Local gentry and wealthy people have also made donations. Li Houji donated 2,000 yuan, Wu Jichang donated 500 yuan, and County Magistrate Yang donated 400 yuan. In addition, local personnel also initiated a disaster relief drama, with all expenses borne by the initiators, which can net 3,000 yuan. Other entertainment venues and entertainment groups have generously donated. However, after the major disaster in Xuzhou, they have all been affected, and there is still an urgent need for donations from other places to save the disaster victims. After Shen and Han finished their investigation, they went to investigate the seven counties. (24th)

Large-Scale Bandit Suppression by Troops Stationed in Western Anhui

Zha Bu Correspondence: The territory of Huoqiu and Lu'an in western Anhui is complex with mountains, so the Red bandits have been hiding in it, and they have not been completely eliminated so far. However, the various armies are still carrying out suppression. For example, the military authorities in the Yejiaji, Balitan, Baitaban, Wangjialoulou, Gujiadian, Hongjiaji, and Chongxingji areas in the southern part of Huoqiu, which have been reduced to Red areas, believe that the Song Shike unit of the temporarily compiled 2nd Brigade stationed in Huoqiu lacks training, so the county seat of Huoqiu has been in danger of being lost several times. Therefore, the independent brigade Zheng Tingzhen unit of the 32nd Division Liang Guanying was specially dispatched from Lu'an to Huoqiu to assist in the suppression of bandits. It is reported that the Zheng unit has recently joined forces with the local security regiment of Sun Gengshan and Yao, etc., and advanced from Huoqiu to the bandit area to search and suppress. They captured a lot along the way. When they attacked Danjiapu, the bandits were in a terrible state, but they still stubbornly resisted by the river. The local farmers took the initiative to join forces with the Red Band and White Tassel Spear Society to cross the river to assist in the attack.

The bandit forces were unable to resist and retreated one after another. The military and civilians took advantage of the victory to pursue and kill countless bandits. Yuan Jingfu, head of the Huoqiu Special Zone Joint Defense and Countryside Clearing Special Service Regiment, also led his team across the river to assist in the attack. In Lu'an, the Red bandits entrenched in the Donglianghekou area gathered more than a thousand people a week ago and crossed the river from Panjiawei to attack the Wangjiangwan anti-communist regiment. The leader of the regiment, Zhou Chengqing, led his team to fight head-on. After about an hour of fighting, they were unable to resist due to their weakness. They lured the bandits to the vicinity of Qingshan and urgently reported to the Wang and Liu brigade leaders of the 46th Division stationed in Subu for assistance. Wang and Liu rushed to help after receiving the report. The bandits were caught off guard and were defeated. They retreated to Lianghekou. The bandits were scrambling to cross the river to escape when the government army had already chased after them. They swept the bandit ships with machine guns, and many ships were hit and sunk. Many bandits drowned, so they were already in disarray. Moreover, the bandit leader Mao Zhengchu has been shot dead by the pseudo-division commander Xiao Fang, so the bandit army is on the verge of collapse. The Lu'an County Government believes that the Red bandits are spreading within the territory, and there are latent dangers everywhere. They have now issued special orders to the anti-communist regiments and security regiments in various towns, townships, and districts to strictly clear the countryside to eliminate the bandit scourge. (August 23rd)

Wuhu Fast Mail

The Wuhu County Education Fund has always relied heavily on surcharges on farmland. This year, the polder fields were almost completely flooded, and the education fund is on the verge of bankruptcy. Yesterday, County Education Director Yu and others convened a county-wide education administrative conference and decided that in addition to apportioning a small amount of the original education fund, they would also organize an education fund relief committee to raise funds. In terms of thrift, they will close schools with poor performance, merge classes, stop recruiting new students, and reduce administrative expenses.

The Wuhu Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee recently held a meeting and resolved that the Wuhu rapeseed, which was originally sold to the Japanese, should be banned from export. The resale of Japanese goods to the mainland by various merchants is also strictly prohibited from export, and the industry workers are instructed not to transport them.

The water level here has risen more than five inches in the past few days. The Hankou branch of the Bank of China telegraphed the Wuhu branch, saying that there will be two feet of floodwater passing through Wuhu. Please pay attention to raising the warehouses. The water depth on Erjie Road and other places has reached more than four feet, and people cannot live in the houses. The number of displaced people is increasing day by day. All traffic can only be done by boats. The Public Security Bureau has opened boat registration and charges a handling fee of 5 jiao and 3 jiao. However, these people are all flood refugees and rickshaw pullers who have changed their professions and are extremely poor, so public opinion is against it.

Most of the industries in the Wuhu market have been suspended since the flood. The Public Security Bureau also has no way to collect the shop rent that it relies on to maintain itself. Bureau Director Zhao Jingshi invited the Chamber of Commerce and the banking industry to hold a meeting. As a result, they borrowed 10,000 yuan from the banking industry to meet the urgent need and will collect and repay it after the market recovers. (23rd)

Education News

Important News

Students from Unregistered and Closed Schools Allowed to Transfer to Appropriate Grades

The Ministry of Education, based on the report from the Nanjing Municipal Education Bureau, stated that 13 private secondary schools requested that students from unregistered or closed schools be allowed to transfer to appropriate grades and be given academic status to encourage talent. The Ministry of Education instructed to check Article 17 of the Provisional Regulations for Secondary Schools, which stipulates that the entrance qualifications for junior high school are graduation from elementary school, and the entrance qualifications for senior high school are graduation from junior high school. If there are no two qualifications mentioned above, those with equivalent levels who pass the examination may also be admitted. Students from unregistered or closed schools who apply for admission may be admitted if they pass the examination and have equivalent levels. However, they must follow the Ministry's Order No. 854 of 1919, and the bureau will determine the proportion of students admitted to the total number of new students.

Request to Change the Length of Medical Specialty Studies to Three Years

The central government has decided to universally establish agricultural, medical, and engineering specialty schools in all provinces and cities, implementing plans for this as well as for establishing secondary agricultural and industrial schools. The duration of medical specialty studies was changed to four years. Subsequently, the Ministry of Education, based on recommendations from the Medical Education Committee, requested that the duration of pharmaceutical specialty school studies be limited to three years, plus one year of internship. The reasons are: (1) Given that medical schools are divided into two levels as a premise, the difference in duration between medical specialty schools and medical colleges should be at least two years; (2) Medical specialty schools aim to meet the urgent needs of the present, and reducing the duration of studies by one year would be more convenient for both the schools and the students. If the duration of studies for medical specialty schools is set at four years, the internship period should seemingly be included within that time. After the Ministry of Education submitted the situation to the Executive Yuan, it is rumored that approval will be granted.

Local News

Covenant for Fellows of the Vocational Education Society to Use National Goods

The Chinese Vocational Education Society, recognizing the dangers of economic aggression by the great powers, previously held a national vocational education discussion meeting in Zhenjiang. The meeting featured a proposal to adopt domestic goods, which was unanimously approved by the attending representatives. Recently, the staff of the society's office department have specially formulated five articles of covenant to ensure compliance. In addition to all staff members signing the covenant, it will also be circulated to all affiliated organizations, and it is planned to widely encourage all members within the country to implement it. The society's circular and covenant are recorded below. It says: Respected Sirs, the other day, the colleagues attended the vocational education discussion meeting in Zhenjiang, and the Zhenjiang organs set up a banquet to invite them to the Chamber of Commerce at that time, and the patriotic atmosphere permeated the whole hall. It was decided that all organs and staff members will uniformly use domestic goods in the future, and no matter how crude the domestic goods are, they should be used as much as possible. Our Vocational Education Society has already initiated it in the past, and should follow the principle of giving priority to righteousness. It will be implemented immediately, persistently and strictly, and from advocating the use of domestic goods, it will be transformed into using domestic goods and revitalizing domestic goods. This is not only fulfilling the duties of a single citizen, but also the rise and fall of the nation's future depends on it. The covenant is drafted as written on the left. If you agree, please sign your name.

Covenant of the Chinese Vocational Education Society

(1) From the date of signing this covenant, the fellows of the society, individuals and their families, pledge to use domestic goods for all items used for clothing, food, housing and transportation, and not to use Japanese goods. (2) In addition to using domestic goods and not using Japanese goods for themselves and their families, the fellows of the society shall also be responsible for persuading relatives, friends and neighbors to act in a unified manner. (3) Fellows of the Society shall advocate that all items used by the Society should be domestic goods. If it is found that Japanese goods have been mistakenly purchased, the clerk should be informed to pay attention. Only if it is absolutely necessary to use foreign goods can a proposal be submitted to a meeting for decision. (4) Within the last year, the fellows of the Society may propose opinions on promoting domestic goods and revitalizing domestic goods at the office meeting held on the first Monday of each month for public discussion. (5) The effective period of this covenant shall be limited to one year for the time being, that is, from August of the 20th year of the Republic of China to July of the 21st year. After the expiry date, another one will be formulated.

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, in order to promote civic sports, cultivate citizens' healthy physique, and select representatives from this city for the 20th National Games, has specifically scheduled the second Municipal Sports Games from September 12 to 18 this year. The sports games regulations and competition rules have been approved by the Municipal Government and are recorded below.

Shanghai Second City Games Regulations

Article 1 The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau promotes municipal sports to cultivate

The Municipal Government of Shanghai organized the second city games to cultivate citizens' physical fitness and select representatives from the city for the 20th National Games.

Article 2 All students and citizens of the city's secondary schools and above, except those who are engaged in sports as a profession, may participate.

Article 3 The opening date of this conference is scheduled to be from September 12 to 18 of the 20th year. If necessary, the chairman may decide to extend it.

Article 4 This conference will be held at the Chinese National Sports Association Chinese Sports Field on Lao Shenfu Road.

Article 5 This conference shall have one president, one vice president, and one secretary-general to preside over all conference affairs.

Article 6 This conference is divided into two departments: administrative affairs and competition. The administrative department shall have one director and one clerk. It shall be divided into eleven sections, including document, editing, layout, reception, discipline, publicity, general affairs, awards, transportation, and medical affairs. Each section shall have one director and several section members. The competition department shall have one director and one clerk. It shall be divided into three sections: registration, distribution, and venue. Each section shall have one director and several section members. There will also be athletic, soccer, basketball, tennis, volleyball, baseball, swimming, national arts, and eight committees. Each committee shall have one chairman and several members.

Article 7 The officials of this conference shall be nominated by the Director of Education and reported to the Mayor for approval. They shall not be paid salaries or allowances.

Article 8 This conference shall be cancelled immediately after the expiration of the meeting period. All handling of conference affairs shall be reported to the Municipal Government by the Education Bureau for record.

Article 9 These regulations shall be implemented from the date of approval and promulgation by the Municipal Government.

Free Talk

World Trivia

— Sea Guest

An Unusually Large Bed

The most famous bed in England is the Great Bed of Ware, recently displayed in the Victoria and Albert Museum. This large bed was previously used for many years at the Crown Inn in Ware, Hertfordsbire, and was later moved to another hotel. It is indeed an antique.

In old English inns, it seems that large beds were commonly used, with many travelers sleeping on the same bed. For example, the White Hart Inn in Scole, Norfolk, had an unusually large bed that could accommodate as many as forty people. This can be considered an unprecedentedly large bed in bed history.

The origin of large beds is very simple. According to Bishop of Portsmouth, Bishopofportsmouth, his great-grandfather was an Irish gentleman who had a large bed in the billiard room of his residence that could comfortably sleep eight people. It was specially designed for guests, because after their dinner, they played billiards for pleasure. When they wanted to go back, the outside of the door was all swampy and it was inconvenient to travel at night, so they stayed on that big bed for one night. Later, hotels adopted this method and prepared large beds. But in the twentieth century, travelers preferred to stay in a room alone, and these large beds were abandoned.

Eulogy for General Xuanwei

— Tao Zaidong

General Xuanwei, the late Jiang Zun, courtesy name Boqi, passed away at the age of fifty on the eighth day of the eighth month of this year while residing in Shanghai. Alas! During the Xinhai Revolution, you were the second governor of Zhejiang Province. Your successor was Zhu Xingwu, for whom I served as the secretary of the Xingwu administrative office, so I knew much of your actions. In the fourth year of the Republic [1915], I was sent to the old capital on official business. At that time, you were a general in the General's Office, and we had a very pleasant conversation. When I was heading south, you hosted a farewell banquet. After the drinking, you and Zhu Baozan secretly confided in me, telling me that the Five-Route Memorial Case would inevitably lead to the establishment of an imperial system. You said, "I must leave Beijing and return to mobilize the people of Zhejiang to prepare for a response." Not long after, the Chuoan Society was indeed established, and you also drifted away into seclusion. In the sixth and seventh years of the Republic [1917-1918], I served as magistrate of Zhuji, your hometown. In my governance and reforms, I often received your assistance. Elder Guan Yun especially praised and supported me. When the supervisory order was issued to cut back veterans' pensions, I submitted a petition against it, arguing with the governor, and narrowly escaped censure because of your family connection. Later, police officer Si told me, "Qi Xi did not blame Shu Xiang for not apologizing because he was acting in the public interest." Between the thirteenth and fourteenth years of the Republic [1924-1925], when Qi Xie and Lu Yongxiang were at odds, Sun Xia governed Zhejiang. You were invited to Hangzhou to attend a welcome meeting. At that time, I was magistrate of Hangzhou. After the public banquet, we had a private meeting. Knowing the hardship of the chief magistrate in providing for everything, you suggested, "Why not seek a transfer?" I quoted Liu Zhiji, the historian, saying, "Being treated worse than a slave by Zhou Gong and Confucius," and said, "Today's county magistrates are like this. What choice is there in going to another county?" You were silent. The following year, I resigned and made a living as a writer in Shanghai. I met you at the funeral of Mr. Zhou. We sat together with Chen Jikan, Xu Guiqing, Yu Tieshan, and others from Zhuji. You repeatedly praised my integrity and ability, and there was an intention to encourage me to return to office. But you did not know that I was like a weary bird returning to the clouds, with no intention of leaving my secluded life. I have the illness of Tao Yuanming, so I am lazy. Even if relatives and friends come to visit, I do not return the visit, and often do not see them for years. But Xingru from my family, who has been traveling with you, tells me that you have been practicing Buddhism devoutly, and your household is serene. When you were seriously ill, your friend Li Wuning visited you three or four times a day. Each time, he would leave five hundred or even a thousand gold coins for medical expenses. On the day of your death, he added another thousand gold coins to buy a coffin and shroud. Otherwise, you would have had no means for burial due to your poverty. Therefore, everyone praises Wuning, and I especially admire that a man of integrity befriends another man of integrity. You were a pioneer in the revolution and a respected elder in the military. Father and son were both accomplished in civil and military affairs, and your name was highly respected in the southeast. Fifty is the age when the ancients took office. How could the concession be a place where we wished to end our days? Yet, you died of poverty and illness, which is heartbreaking. Reflecting on our lifelong friendship, I regret that I am old and my talent has faded, and I cannot write an inscription of gold and stone to commemorate you. While lamenting the deceased, I also reflect on myself. I have composed an elegiac poem to express my sorrow. The poem says: "The revolution has not yet succeeded, and you have died young. It makes heroes fill their sleeves with tears. As an official, I knew I was incompetent, but you wrongly praised my integrity and ability. How can I compare to Marquis Fuqianqu?"

Life is Twenty-One Years

— Wang Yanjin

According to the statistics of the world's human age table, the age of ordinary people is approximately from fifty to seventy years old. Averaging this out, we can assume it to be sixty years old. Now, let's subtract the time spent on meals, sleep, and rest to calculate the actual time for work.

1. Education time: 15 years. 2. Rest time: 7.5 years. (Assuming 50 rest days per year, and 10 days for illness.) 3. Meal time: 4 years and 8 months. (Calculating 3 hours per day). 4. Sleep time: 10 years and 11 months. (Sleeping at 10 pm and waking up at 5 am.) 5. Post-meal rest time: 18 months. (Resting for 10 minutes after each meal.)

Excluding the above five items, what remains is the time for work in life. Calculating carefully, it does not even amount to twenty-one years and one month. Compatriots, the time in life is so short, and our mission is so heavy. We cannot allow for even a moment of negligence, laziness, or procrastination. Let's all work hard! I hope that friends and families will cut out this table and use it as our motto.

A Record of Watching Quail Fights

— Jian Fu

In a Yuan palace poem by Zhu Youdun of the Song Dynasty, it says, "When the Mid-Autumn Festival approaches, we cut velvet flowers and incite quail fights." The custom of quail fighting has been around for a long time and did not originate today. However, in ancient times, this was done as a game, while now it is done for gambling. That is the difference. The trend of quail fighting is prevalent in Jiangbei, with Hao County being the most prominent. A good quail can be worth over a hundred taels of gold, and the stakes for betting can amount to tens of thousands. Many middle-class families go bankrupt because of this. It is even more extravagant than the cricket fights of the wealthy. Last autumn, I stayed in Hao County, during the time of quail fighting. Due to the strict prohibition by the authorities, it was not possible to openly set up arenas for gambling; instead, it was done in private residences. Before the fight, the quail's physique is first examined, and then the betting value is discussed to ensure fairness. Quail breeders often keep the quail in brocade pouches, with an oval-shaped wooden ring at the bottom to prevent the quail from being crushed. Quail born in early spring are called "Bai Bi," while those born after autumn are called "Zao Tu." Zao Tu have the most venomous beaks, which Bai Bi cannot withstand. Therefore, those who raise Bai Bi are often unwilling to have them fight Zao Tu. Such is the reason. The fighting method involves placing a large bamboo basket on the ground and putting the quail inside from the pouch. Grain is then scattered in the basket. When the quail see the grain, they fight over it. During the fight, they each raise their wings, making a "woo-woo" sound. The duration of the fight can be several minutes or even tens of minutes. If they are evenly matched, it can last for quite some time. Exhausted, they each rest for a while, glaring at each other like angry frogs. After a while, one of them looks down, wanting to peck at the grain. The other suddenly pounces forward. Then the fierce fighting resumes. After this final battle, the victory and defeat are determined, and the betting stakes are also judged. At this time, the winning quail grabs the food, and the winning person grabs the money, obtaining what is called the spoils of war. Their joy knows no bounds. The losing quail jumps out of the basket, not daring to re-enter, and the losing person feels sorry for the loss of money, filled with shame and anger, looking quite disheveled. The transformations of people and things at this point are truly a sight to behold. The reporter is deeply moved by gambling with quail fights. The quail are pure. When they are in the wild, they call out to each other when they find food and gather together when they hear the sound. They lie together during the day and fly together at night, without any sense of gain or loss. What is the meaning of fighting? But after being raised by humans, they fight each other when they see food and become hostile when they hear sounds. They treat the pouch as their territory and the bamboo basket as their battlefield. Because of the fight over millet today, they forget the righteousness of being in the wild. How superficial they are! The change in the nature of things is so rapid, which is also strange.

Anecdotes from the North Station

— Lanxi

Having read the "Anecdotes from the North Station" by Qi Jun published in yesterday's newspaper, all the sections are true. However, there are still matters that are both important and crucial that were not mentioned. I am supplementing them here.

This flood has affected sixteen provinces, a rare catastrophe unseen in a hundred years. It is indeed a harsh punishment from heaven to the people. We, who reside in Shanghai, enjoy gentle breezes and warm sunshine, with calm waves. Compared to the refugees who are bearing the brunt of the disaster, who lack food, clothing, and shelter, it is no less than heaven and hell. However, everyone has a heart of compassion. After reading the reports of the devastation, can we not feel a surge of sympathy? Therefore, the two Railway Bureau directors, Mr. Guo, initiated a fundraising campaign for the national flood disaster on both railways and jointly formulated fundraising measures with key members of the two railways. All railway staff with salaries below fifty yuan are to donate fifteen percent; those below one hundred yuan, twenty percent; and those above one hundred yuan, twenty-five percent. If railway staff have any other suggestions, they can submit them within three days. When it comes to benevolence, people with good intentions all have the same heart. The severity of the flood is fiercer than poisonous snakes and fierce tigers. Those who have not been affected can imagine it. How can those who are well-fed and living comfortably bear to hear countless suffering compatriots crying out for food without showing compassion? The staff of the two railways, calculated according to these figures, can collect more than eighty thousand yuan. However, it is still like a drop in the bucket. It is hoped that all Shanghai residents will fulfill their sense of self-love and self-interest, and donate according to their abilities. Then, a little effort can accumulate into a great achievement, and the disaster victims will receive boundless blessings.

Short News. The Weiya Restaurant, in light of the severe floods affecting various provinces this year, a rare occurrence in nearly a century, the entire staff of the main store and its branches, both labor and management, will make a charitable effort today. All proceeds from business, plus small tips and rewards, will be transferred to the Flood Relief Association to aid disaster relief. Although it is like a drop in the bucket, many large stores are full of benevolent people, fulfilling the natural duty of humanity. Continuing charitable efforts may well accumulate into a great achievement. (Initial)

Travels in India (91)

— Linghua

January 1, 20th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1931]. Staying at the residence of lawyer Mu Keji in Sllahabadu, Allahabad City. In the morning, I rode a bicycle to tour the woods. The air in the north of the city is fresh and the roads are wide, shaded by large trees, far superior to other cities. To the east is the sacred water of the Ganges River, where for thousands of years, seven women have been baptized to repent for their sins. It is the Jordan River of India. Today, I went to the home of a wealthy old woman with lawyer Mu. She was extremely rich but very stingy, and deeply religious. She bowed at every temple along the way, but would not easily give a penny to the rickshaw puller, making one think of the uselessness of superstition. Traveling east for about five miles, near the train tracks, there are rows of large trees with pale bark, called Asutar. This tree occupies a great position in India, and those who worship it are numerous, with the same need as worshiping cows. It is also called the "Mother Tree," being the wife of a certain tree. No Indian dares to harm the Mother Tree. The male tree can be used for medicine and has a wide range of uses. People use it but forget to love it. However, the Mother Tree has no use, but Indians worship and protect it. Whoever dares to harm the Mother Tree will be surrounded by a crowd and fought to the death. It is like someone daring to kill a cow in an Indian religious city, then the Indians will gather and kill that person, as if protecting their mother. I asked its scholars and university professors about the principles of protecting cows, and they all replied, "Our entire family has grown up eating milk since childhood. Having eaten its milk, to eat its meat would be without heavenly principles and conscience, which Indians do not do." I was deeply touched by their words. How India knows to repay kindness! Observing the worship of Mother Trees and Mother Cows in India, I realized the origin of the Buddhist scriptures on repaying kindness. This good thought of repaying kindness has already planted good roots in East Asia and will surely spread throughout the globe in the future. Only then can we hope for peace. India is a nation of maternal religion and maternal culture.

Around noon, I saw that each temple, large and small, had an object placed in the middle of the hall. The large ones were like millstones, and the small ones were like plates or cups. The largest were seven or eight feet tall, standing like cones, about a foot thick. Their shape was like a stick. No temple was without this object, and they were all made of stone. Some temples had multiple types. I had long been suspicious of this. Why did they resemble the sexual organs of men and women in coitus? I had long heard that Rome had the custom of worshiping the male genitalia. Master Wanhui said that India had the custom of worshiping reproductive organs. Could this be the object? However, in the cities, it was difficult to observe the temples because there were many people and the rooms were dark, making it difficult to distinguish. After visiting the countryside, I realized that they were everywhere under the clear blue sky. I began to understand that Indian religion is the religion of worshiping the sexual intercourse of men and women. This is generally true throughout India, but the sects are largely the same with minor differences. But its form is so obvious and clear. I asked the Indians what this object was. The Indians said, "Mahadeva," meaning the great god or great heaven. The name "Great Heaven" is seen in Buddhist scriptures. Men and women named "Great Heaven" are everywhere. They believe that this is the root of all gods, and all gods have spouses, being the source of life for humans and all things and the natural world. This source comes from the great god, so it must be worshiped, meaning heaven and earth, father and mother. However, for thousands of years, philosophers have added profound and mysterious explanations to it, making the learning so incomprehensible and eternally impossible to understand. Like the Chinese Xiantian Taoism, it also talks about the origins of human reproduction and all things in the world. Confucianism's Book of Changes talks about yin and yang, Taiji, and the eight trigrams, where father and mother, men and women, give birth to each other. There is nothing strange about this. However, I find it quite strange that Indians worship the naked sexual organs of men and women.

Random Notes from the Northeast Inspection (2)

— Liu Sui Jiu

There are three villages with separate residences for professors: (1) Dongxin Village, (2) Xixin Village, and (3) Nanxin Village. Each village has dozens of residences. The houses are equipped with steam heating pipes, hot and cold water pipes, and porcelain toilets and bathtubs. Each house is estimated to be worth about ten thousand yuan. There is also a radio station, a sports field worth three hundred thousand yuan, a foundry, and a weaving factory. There is also a science museum worth two hundred and forty thousand yuan and a large library with construction costs estimated at three hundred thousand yuan. The entire school currently holds approximately over 70,000 books, valued at over 1.28 million yuan. The College of Science and Engineering currently has six to seven thousand kinds of machinery and chemicals, over 16,000 pieces of equipment, and 530 working machines in the factory, along with tens of thousands of tools. There are currently over 200 faculty and staff members and over 2,000 male and female students. The school's annual budget has increased from 439,000 yuan to over 1.3 million yuan. The scale is rare in the country.

(3) The Magnificence of Beiling

To the north of Northeast University is Beiling, the mausoleum of the former Qing Emperor Taizong. The architecture is magnificent, similar to Beiping Park. There are large pine forests to the east and west. Sitting and sipping tea, one feels transported to another world. Every day, Chinese and foreign tourists are endless. However, most tourists only see it as a scenic spot or a park. I am particularly interested in the love affair between Taizong's Empress Wen and Hong Chengchou, which people still enjoy discussing to this day. When I first arrived in Shenyang, I stayed at the YMCA at Dananmen, which was the place where Hong Chengchou was imprisoned at that time. A woman with great strategies, Taizong relied on her internal assistance to win the world. This is rare in ancient and modern history.

Taizong's mausoleum is called "Zhaoling." Beiling is a popular name. The Japanese have specialized in the study of its architecture and have written "Illustrated Explanation of Zhaoling in Fengtian," which is a total of 149 pages. On November 2nd last year, the Fengtian Library established by the Japanese held an exhibition. I was invited by the library director, Mr. Eto Toshio, to visit. I saw rubbings of the Tablet of Divine Merit and Sacred Virtue of Emperor Wen of Taizong in Zhaoling, and rubbings of the Tablet of Divine Merit and Sacred Virtue of Emperor Gao of Taizu in "Fuling" (i.e., Dongling). The inscriptions are in Chinese, Manchu, and Mongolian. I have visited various places to find these rubbings but have not been able to see them. Unexpectedly, I saw them in a Japanese library, which is fortunate. I also saw displayed in the library German-published photographic reproductions of such Manchu and Mongolian inscriptions, as well as various reduced versions of the tablets of Lama temples (such as the large tablet in four languages of Chinese, Manchu, Mongolian, and Tibetan in the Yonghe Temple in Beiping). They were very exquisite, and I was surprised by the precision of foreigners' research on our country's history. Therefore, when we visit Zhaoling, how can we merely stop at visiting a park and sipping tea?

It is said that Emperor Wen of Taizong of the Qing Dynasty was named Huang Taiji, the eighth son of Emperor Gao of Taizu, Nurhaci, and the brother of Prince Regent Dorgon. He died at the age of fifty-two, after reigning for seventeen years. After his death, his ninth son, Shunzhi, succeeded to the throne. His mausoleum is about ten miles from the city. The terrain is excellent. The Liao River curves to the right, and the Hun River wraps around to the left. Mountains are built with earth. The towers and battlements are towering, and the palaces are magnificent, comparable to palaces. In front of the Long'en Gate is the largest blue square brick, called "Danchi." It is said that officials of the nine Qing departments all sat here in order of rank. There is a line in Du Fu's poem "Facing the Danchi alone, the sun has not yet set," referring to this. Inside the Long'en Hall are the spirit tablets of Taizong and Empress Wen. The carved beams and painted rafters in the hall are exceptionally exquisite. In front of the main door of the hall is a piece of long, smooth green stone, about seven or eight feet long and three or four feet wide. The colors are brilliant and dazzling, truly a rare item. The steps connecting to the green stone in front have three white gemstone steps, with a smooth and lustrous stone quality and radiating precious light. To the west of the white gemstones is a piece of lapis lazuli in a rectangular form. Qing officials of the fourth rank used this kind of gemstone as the lapis lazuli top bead.

US Cotton Rebound After Shorts Covered: Yesterday, US cotton rose due to good news from Liverpool, and short positions were covered due to fears of a rebound. Futures rose by 18 to 23 points, and spot prices rose by 20 points. British cotton futures rose by 11-12 points, and spot prices rose by 8 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices rose by 5 points. Indian cotton rose due to better opening prices in Liverpool and purchases by Japanese merchants. Pingguoer rose by 1 rupee, Aomula rose by 1.75 rupees, and Bailuoxi rose by 0.5 rupees. The original telegram is recorded on the left (24th telegram).

Rice Prices Rise Sharply by One Yuan

Due to the storm and rain yesterday, no boats could reach the South Market, and the inventory in the port was weak. In the morning, the number of people visiting the market was still quite large, and the route out of this street was more active than the previous market. Prices of various goods rose sharply, and people were panicked. Thin rice and thick japonica rice both rose by about one yuan. Although there was little early rice on the market, the situation also increased by 6 or 7 jiao. Superior grade rice was scarce, and customers continued to buy nearly 1,000 shi. The opening prices were all up by 4 or 5 jiao. New japonica rice and rice affected by weather were scarce.

Sources for Xinzha West Road were scarce, and city and rural transactions were not active. According to letters from Wuxi, the market for brown rice is increasing. According to this situation, prices of japonica and early and late indica rice rose by 5 or 6 jiao. Top-grade, reed-tip, port-tip, new japonica, and glutinous rice all rose by 4 or 5 jiao. The inventory of foreign rice was weak, and foreign firms continued to buy, and the opening price rose sharply by 3 jiao. River factories opened about 6,200 to 6,300 dan of various goods.

Foreign Rice Prices Rise Sharply

Yesterday's foreign rice market situation: Although transactions were not very active, the market was quite good. Warehouses on this street had a good appetite. Because Shanghai has been hit by storms and rain, the price of white rice from downstream areas has skyrocketed, with the northern market rising by one yuan and the southern market rising by 6 or 7 jiao. Therefore, they were very active in buying foreign rice, and the price suddenly rose sharply. 1,000 bags of No. 2 Saigon were offered at 13.5 yuan, and 300 bags of small-grain rice were offered at 12.95 yuan. In addition, 170 bags of Jiangxi machine rice were offered at 14.8 yuan, all bought by warehouses on this street. A telegram for foreign rice was approved to ship several hundred tons of small-grain rice immediately at a price of 6 taels and 8.5 qian.

Storm Creates Rise in Flour Prices

Yesterday's flour market: After the opening of the market in the morning, the prices of each month were generally hovering. Foreign wheat quotations had fallen slightly by 3 or 4 jiao, causing the market to be very quiet and transactions were few. Until the afternoon opening, sentiment was excited and prices rose sharply. Due to the sudden storm and heavy rain, and the predictions that Shanghai will also have a flood, the buying interest for near months was strong. The quantity of traders vying to buy from domestic gangs was extremely large. The buying interest for September, October, and November was the strongest, and the price increases were also drastic. This kind of price increase was purely caused by the storm. If the rain stops and the weather clears, sentiment should return to normal. As a result, the current month rose by 1.5 cents compared to the previous day, September rose by 2.25 cents, October rose by 3 cents, November rose by 2.75 cents, December rose by 3.25 cents, and February rose by 2.5 cents.

Wheat Market Turns Firm in Afternoon, Near Months Uniquely Weak

Yesterday's wheat futures market: After the opening of the market in the morning, the quotations for foreign wheat for each month were still not good, and the market was still flat. Until the afternoon opening, sentiment became excited due to the storm and rain. Domestic gangs successively purchased far-term months, and the market turned firm. Due to the settlement relationship of the current month, and because those preparing for delivery on the short side were between one and two hundred vehicles, and factories were not active, it was forcibly suppressed, and it felt slightly lower than the previous day. As a result, the current month fell by 1 cent compared to the previous day, and September to December each rose by 5 cents, and January rose by 3 cents. The spot wheat market turned quiet, and factories only responded. A total of over 1,000 bags of Kunshan and Pukou wheat were opened in the city, and the price did not fluctuate.

Silk and Tea Japanese Merchants Replenish Stocks at Low Prices

Yesterday, the silk market in Shanghai foreign firms still showed no improvement. Factory operations in New York are still at a standstill. Yesterday morning's silk report from Lyon, England, also showed no turn to Shanghai. Only Japanese firms replenished factory supplies at low prices, but the asking prices were not high, and factories' willingness to sell remained weak. Yesterday, only Mitsui bought 30 bales of medium Shanghai white from a factory, and Kechang bought 20 bales of yellow coarse silk. Prices remained firm.

50 Pieces of New Silk Factory Cargo Arrived in Hangzhou

Various silk factories in Hangzhou are bearing the foreign banks' monthly contract silk sales. Currently, because of the approach of the contract settlement, they are delivering the spot silk to Shanghai. Yesterday, 50 pieces of new factory silk from Wei Cheng and other factories were transported from Hangzhou by the Shanghai-Hangzhou train to prepare for settlement at the end of the month.

Autumn Cocoon Feeding Volume in Linping Not Weak

Smooth Incubation...Good Collection of Ants

Farmers in the Linping area have suffered losses in both spring and summer cocoons this year, and their willingness to raise autumn cocoons is quite strong. They pre-purchased a large number of improved varieties and started hatching. The weather was clear and pleasant, and the incubation was smooth, and the collection of ants was good. The feeding volume increased by about 30% compared to the summer cocoons.

Gongxi Green Tea Sales to Europe Turn Smooth

Yesterday, the Shanghai foreign tea market saw slightly sluggish transactions of Zhenmei green tea from Wuyuan, Tunxi, and other areas. Except for the tip-picking category, which was still selling well to France, the rest were deserted. However, the Gongxi category saw some interest from British firms Jinlong, Baochang, Xiehe, Fushi, and others, as well as the China Tea Company. The Russian Aid Association also had some sporadic demand, and transactions were not quiet. The market price was unchanged from before. The market conditions for other items such as Zhenmei and Xiumei were slightly sluggish.

New Autumn Woolen Cloth Sales Activated for Piece Goods

As the new autumn season arrives and the weather gradually turns clear, the sales of woolen goods continue, and the market is gradually activating. In addition to the Hankou and Nanhua gangs, other Shanghai firms are also purchasing. Commonly used blue-grey plain serge, Huate woolen cloth, Huate woolen cloth in various mixed colors, Yuanzhigong, as well as Sea Tiger, Leopard Skin, Qiang, shoe felt cloth, and Maildeng thick woolen cloth all had transactions, and the original numbers of scattered pieces were opened for sale every day, and their sales were quite active.

Hardware Transactions Increasingly Quiet in Storm

Since the autumn, the sluggish sales and scarce practical applications of hardware have been rare in previous years. However, due to the impact of floods in various places, or the disturbances of soldiers and bandits, the period when autumn sales were activated in previous years saw a steady stream of purchasers, but this year there are very few. Because of this, the market is in a state of panic, and although standard grades are being maintained with great effort, the quiet business means that there is an appearance of strength but inner weakness. Furthermore, yesterday's storm and heavy rain caused fewer people to come to the market, so the goods opened for sale were even scarcer. It is estimated that over 200 dan of 7.5% British steel plates were sold yesterday at a price of 6 taels and 3.5 qian. 300-400 dan of No. 16 to No. 20 new lead wire were estimated at 13 taels and 2.5 qian. Various customer gangs were very diligent in purchasing No. 14 colored goods, and the market price was 12 taels and 2.5 qian. There were only sporadic transactions of American galvanized iron and black iron sheets. Although the Northern gangs were still inquiring about garden lead wire, the number of transactions was still scarce. In addition, although there were slightly more iron products opened for sale yesterday, the market did not fluctuate much.
