British Public Bus Drivers' Mediation Breaks Down

The Company Proposes Five Conditions for Resuming Work

Workers' Congress Resolves to Continue Strike

After the strike of all ticket sellers of the British Public Bus Company, the company still reluctantly operated routes 1, 2, 5, 9, and the AB special express yesterday. The mediation by the drivers broke down. The company proposed five conditions for resuming work. The workers held a congress yesterday, and the labor community actively provided assistance. The various situations yesterday are recorded below. Mediation Breakdown: At 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, the British Public Bus Company drivers, based on the resolution of the delegates' congress, sent three representatives to the British China Public Bus Co., Ltd. on the Bund of the Great Horse Road to mediate on behalf of the ticket sellers' nine conditions of treatment. As a result, the manager completely rejected all nine conditions and put forward five conditions for resuming work. The three representatives believed that the company was relying on imperialist forces to excessively oppress the workers and were very angry and withdrew, resulting in the breakdown of the mediation.

Company Conditions: The company proposed the following conditions for resuming work: (1) Ticket sellers who wish to serve in the company as a result of the strike must submit a list on the morning of the 25th of this month; (2) The company may randomly select members from the list and allow them to serve temporarily, which will be announced on the 26th; (3) Those who wish to serve must comply with the following conditions: (a) Regardless of new or old ticket sellers, the monthly salary will start at 20 yuan, and monthly salary increases will be as usual; (b) The 20 yuan deposit will be kept by the company as usual; (c) All previous bonuses will be canceled, and the bonuses for serving members will be calculated as for new members; (d) This company plans to prepare special bonuses to encourage them; (e) Those who violate the company's regulations will be dismissed immediately, and those who disobey the orders of superior staff will also be dismissed; (4) Among the serving members, the company must select them, and after the selection, they must put their fingerprints on it before the review is carried out in order to withdraw them; (5) The selected members must report to this company for service within 24 hours after the formal announcement.

Workers' Congress: After the ticket sellers were dispersed from the Chinese Park the day before yesterday, they held a full workers' congress again at 8:00 AM yesterday morning. More than 190 ticket sellers attended. First, the chairman reported on the company's refusal to negotiate, and the atmosphere was very tense. On the spot, it was decided that: (1) The strike should continue; (2) Severe measures should be taken against the running dogs who undermine the strike; (3) All trade unions in the city should be asked for assistance.

Labor Community Assistance: After all the ticket sellers of the British Public Automobile Company went on strike on the 20th because they could not stand the unreasonable oppression of the imperialist company, the company refused to negotiate and instead dismissed all the workers and proposed conditions for resuming work. The first district water and electricity industry workers' union, the tenth district cotton spinning industry workers' union, the British Concession tram workers' union, etc., all sent representatives to express their condolences, expressing their willingness to act as a backing and fight imperialism to the end.

Petition to the Ministry from the Postal Workers' Union

Regarding the request to amend the Postal Administration Organization Law

A petition from the Shanghai Postal Workers' Union and the Postal Employees' Union to the Legislative Yuan, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Communications, regarding the request to amend the Postal Administration Organization Law, states: Since the promulgation of the Postal Administration Organization Law, it has severely disrupted the postal system, profoundly impacting the future of the postal service, causing widespread anxiety. We respectfully and clearly state the obstacles at each point, earnestly hoping that you will consider the difficulties in establishing the postal service and approve a review and amendment to benefit transportation and strengthen the foundation of the postal service. It is our understanding that China's postal organization system has always been considered sound, which is why it has maintained its reputation for over thirty years as a leading state-owned enterprise. Since the success of the revolution and the recovery of postal rights, although there have been many changes in administration, it has not been as disruptive as the current postal system. The Unions have a deep understanding of postal service and would like to clearly state the following: (1) Article 2 of the organization law stipulates one deputy director general, but does not clearly specify that they should be selected from among senior postal directors. According to the current regulations, the director general is comparable to the current general manager, while the deputy director general is comparable to the deputy manager. When postal rights were recovered, Minister Wang of the Ministry of Communications appointed a senior postal director as the general manager. At that time, the general administration regulations stipulated that the general manager and deputy manager must be filled by postal service personnel. Although subsequent acting general managers were not from the postal service, they still relied on the assistance of experienced deputy managers, so there were few obstacles. The current postal regulations still stipulate that the position of deputy manager must be filled by service personnel. It is understood that postal operations are difficult, and measures are not easy, so non-experienced postal personnel are not qualified. The Unions foresaw this and pleaded with the Ministry during the revision of the organization law to retain this inherent good principle of the postal organization to ensure that the hard-earned foundation of China's postal service would not be shaken. This is not only to select and reward postal personnel as a means of advancement, but the recently revised Postal Administration Organization Law by the Ministry suddenly removes the stipulation that the deputy director general should be appointed from postal personnel. The original good principle has no clear provision, causing widespread anxiety. It is believed that this will cause chaos in the postal organization and hinder the development of the postal service. As a matter of fact, the current deputy manager is a senior postal worker and has been appointed as deputy director general by the Ministry of Communications, which shows that the inherent regulations are suitable for the postal situation. However, without clear provisions, changes are difficult to prevent in the future, and cunning people will easily create a path of competition and pursuit. Therefore, we earnestly request the Ministry to approve a review and retention of the inherent principles, and to clearly stipulate that the position of deputy director general should be appointed from senior postal directors. (2) In addition to the General Affairs, Accounting, Business, Inter-Postal, and Supply Departments stipulated in Article 3, the Performance Appraisal and Audit Departments should still be handled by the Postal Administration. The Performance Appraisal Department is responsible for the promotion, demotion, and dismissal of postal personnel, which has always been handled in accordance with the regulations. Tens of thousands of employees rely on this for protection, and the postal foundation can be consolidated. The Audit Department is responsible for reviewing national postal revenue and expenditure and supervising accounting, which has always been strict. Postal finances can be cleared. These two departments are indispensable to the postal service. The new organization law does not stipulate that they must be assigned to other departments. If they are divided and transferred outside the Postal Administration, the entire good system and its system of the postal service will inevitably be broken. The theory is not sound, and the facts are full of obstacles. The consequences are endless and not a blessing for the transportation industry. Therefore, these two departments should still be handled by the Postal Administration to show consistency and strengthen the postal foundation, and should not be divided. (3) Article 4 stipulates that the Postal Administration may set up a chief secretary, which should also be clearly specified to be appointed by senior postal personnel. The chief secretary is comparable to the current head of the secretariat, and their powers are similar. The head of the secretariat and other department heads have always been filled by senior postal personnel. Article 3 of the new organization law also clearly stipulates that the directors and deputy directors of each department should be selected from postal directors and deputy postal directors. The chief secretary has similar powers and should be treated the same. Moreover, their responsibilities are important and cannot be assumed by non-experienced postal personnel. It should be clearly stipulated that the above three points are related to the development of the postal service, the convenience of the transportation industry, and the glory of the country. The Unions serve the postal service and cannot remain silent. In addition to presenting to the Executive Yuan and submitting to the Postal Administration to forward to the Ministry of Communications to request the Ministry to approve a review and amendment, we should submit another document to the Ministry to earnestly consider the postal service, comply with the wishes of the people, and approve a review and amendment of the obstacles in the Postal Administration Organization Law, which is both for public benefit. Furthermore, the position of Postal Inspector is very important. Although it has been appointed by the Ministry of Communications, it has not been clearly stipulated in the organization law, so it should also be requested by the Ministry to amend and clarify it. Respectfully submitted to the Legislative Yuan. Shanghai Postal Workers' Union and Postal Employees' Union, respectfully submitted on August 25th.

Stalled Sale of Housheng Yarn Factory

Due to Provisional Seizure of Xue Baorun's Assets

The sale of the Housheng Yarn Factory has now been declared stalled because, during the sale process, all assets of Xue Baorun, a major dye merchant, were provisionally seized by the court due to a lawsuit filed by his nephews, Xue Jinfu, etc., for asset division, thus causing the stall. Once found, he will request the court to seize them and sue those who privately transfer ownership for compensation. Second Standing Committee Meeting of the Anti-Japanese Association's Inspection Committee

Request to Exempt Resistance to Pharmaceuticals and Raw Materials Under Study

The second Standing Committee Meeting of the Anti-Japanese Association's Inspection Committee was attended by Li Liangyu, Pan Yisan, Yu Yangzhou, Zhou Renqing, Yang Xiongchan, etc., with Ye Jiaxing as the chairman. The following matters were discussed: (1) Yang Chunsheng's response to the Pharmaceutical Association's request to exempt resistance to seven types of pharmaceutical raw materials. Preparatory Meeting of the National Pharmaceutical Industry Association Union Held Yesterday

The representatives of the initiators of the National Pharmaceutical Industry Association Union held their first preparatory meeting yesterday at the Shanghai National Pharmaceutical Industry Association at 100 Beijing Road. Attendees included Zhang Meian from Shanghai, Cheng Diaozi from Nanjing, Li Tiaoyun from Wujin, Bi Huaizhi from Zhenjiang, etc. Zhang Meian was publicly elected as the chairman. The following resolutions were passed: Matters for discussion: 1. Regarding the fact that this preparatory office had previously resolved on March 15 of this year, when representatives of medical and pharmaceutical groups from various regions gathered in the capital, to appoint five comrades, including Meian, Cheng Diaozi, Fang Yiyuan, Hua Huaizhi, and Cao Zhaochu, to be responsible for preparing the National Pharmaceutical Industry Association Union, and designated the Shanghai National Pharmaceutical Industry Association as the preparatory location, with Zhang Meian as the convener of the first preparatory meeting, how should this preparatory office prepare and proceed? Please make a public decision. It was resolved that all preparatory committee members should be listed in the newspaper and a notice should be sent to invite all established pharmaceutical industry associations from various regions to join as initiators to align with the purpose of a united national pharmaceutical industry. 2. Now that this preparatory office has been organized and established, should it be reported to the Ministry of Industry for record? Please make a public decision. It was resolved that it would be reported for record when the number of pharmaceutical industry associations that have joined as initiators accounts for more than half of the country's regions. 3. How should the preparatory funds for this preparatory office be raised? Please make a public decision. It was resolved that the preparatory funds should be shared by all the industry associations that have joined as initiators, and the amount should be determined as follows: Grade A 100 yuan, Grade B 60 yuan, Grade C 30 yuan, Grade D voluntary donation according to their ability. The director of the preparatory office should be fully responsible for the safekeeping of these preparatory funds, which will be directly requested by the relevant industry associations that have pledged to contribute. 4. The format of the official documents of this preparatory office should be specified. Please make a public decision. It was resolved that the official documents of this preparatory office should be headed by the director of the preparatory office and co-signed by all members of the preparatory committee. 5. The temporary seal of this preparatory office should be engraved immediately, but how should its style and wording be determined? Please make a public decision. It was resolved to carve a wooden rectangular seal with the words "Preparatory Committee of the National Pharmaceutical Industry Association Union" and a horizontal rectangular seal with the words "Emblem of the National Pharmaceutical Industry Association Union." The rectangular seal is for general use, and the horizontal rectangular seal is for collecting temporary donations. 6. This preparatory office should hire staff to handle its affairs. Please make a public decision. It was resolved that the director of the preparatory office should hire a secretary, and all clerks and tea servers, etc., should be temporarily concurrently served by those hired by the Shanghai National Pharmaceutical Industry Association, with appropriate stipends. 7. How should the date of the preparatory meeting of this preparatory committee be determined? Please make a public decision. It was resolved that regular meetings should be held once a month, and ad hoc meetings should be convened if necessary.

Road and City Exhibition Tickets Selling Well

Due to Cars and Other Valuable Gifts

The Road and City Exhibition Conference of the China National Road Construction Association held a banquet at the Bank Association on the evening of the 24th of August (i.e., the previous evening) at 7 p.m. to invite prominent figures in Shanghai to discuss the sale of tickets. Those present included Zhao, Chairman of the Association and Vice Minister of Industry, Cao Yunxiang, Director of the Industrial and Commercial Management Association, Lin Kanghou, Director of the General Affairs Section, Zhu Bo, Director of the Finance Section, Yang Nianzu, General Manager of Quan, Zheng Xitao, Executive Director of Wu Shan, and committee members Zhu Shaoping, Shen Zhongjun, Tao Leqin, Yu Sen, Zhao Heqin, Yin Jianfu, Zhu Yangchen, He Dekui, Ren Jinpin, Xu Zhendong, Zhang Zilian, Xiang Kangyuan, as well as Xu Jingren, Chairman of the Relief Committee, and Shanghai merchants Yu Qiaqing, Ye Huijun, Lao Jingxiu, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Guo Bingwen, Wang Boqi, Xu Jiqi, Qin Runqing, Xu Xinliu, Yang Dunfu, Tong Zhenyuan, etc. First, Chairman Zhao delivered the opening speech, followed by Chairman Cao Yunxiang reporting on the preparations and the importance of promoting ticket sales. Lin Kanghou, Yang Nianzu, Xu Jingren, and Yu Qiaqing also gave speeches successively. That evening, those who pledged to sell tickets included Du Yuesheng with 3,000 tickets, Zhang Zilian with 2,000 tickets, and others who pledged to sell 500 or 300 tickets. It was also reported that Mrs. Xiao Zhiji had undertaken to sell 10,000 tickets. Including the 10,000 tickets sold by Minister Wang and other parties, the total number of tickets sold was over 60,000. In addition, it was reported that the association held a full committee meeting at the Bank Association yesterday afternoon to discuss important matters related to the association's progress. There were concrete measures for renting display spaces, selling tickets, and entertainment programs. In addition to more than forty manufacturers from both domestic and foreign countries having signed up for display spaces, each committee member was responsible for contacting at least one manufacturer to come to the exhibition. Each person pledged to sell 500 tickets. The entertainment program has received support from Shanghai celebrities Guo An, Ci Xiuyun, Wang Lianqing, Mrs. Ma, and Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Zhou Jianyun, and Zheng Zhengqiu. It is expected that the performances will be lively. After the meal, the entire group went to the venue in the rain for a photo shoot and then dispersed.

County Government Proclamation to Clean Streets

The County Government issued a proclamation yesterday, stating, "It is important to tidy up roads to improve the appearance of the city. The quality of roads is not only related to the appearance but also to local transportation and public health, which cannot be ignored. It has been found that in the street areas of various districts and towns in this county, melon peels, fruit shells, and garbage are arbitrarily displayed, encroaching on the road surface, obstructing traffic, and detracting from the appearance of the city. Moreover, during this autumn and summer season, dirty and unclean roads are prone to epidemics, which is of great concern to public health. It is necessary to earnestly pay attention to rectification to facilitate transportation and emphasize hygiene. In addition to ordering the Public Security Bureaus to strictly crack down on violations and ordering the district chiefs to pay attention to rectifying the situation at all times, a public notice is hereby issued to inform all the people of the county to be aware of the situation and order them to pay attention to street cleanliness to jointly maintain public health, not to accumulate debris or dump garbage along the street, or to obstruct road administration. Those who dare to arbitrarily disobey will be investigated and dealt with severely. They must all comply with this order."

Male Corpse Found Dead on Song Park Road

An unidentified male corpse was found dead on Song Park Road, Zhongshan Road, Zhabei, yesterday.

The man was about fifty years old and dressed in rags. The landlord Huang Hongsheng of Jin'ertu reported the incident to the local court. Prosecutor Wang and others arrived at the scene and determined that the man had died of an epidemic. The corpse was ordered to be collected by the charity hall.

Lost Boys and Girls Waiting to be Claimed

A local girl named Yu Genxin, fifteen years old, wearing a light white cooked silk short shirt, a dark-colored foreign yarn trousers, black socks, and black shoes, got lost at the intersection of Avenue Joffre and Rue Pellerin at 7:00 PM on the 22nd. Also, an unnamed boy, about seven years old, shirtless, wearing white pants, with a monk's hairstyle, and barefoot, got lost on Route Cardinal Mercier at 9:00 PM on the same day. They were found by the police and taken to the Lujiawan Police Station. When asked about their names and addresses, they could not answer. The police chief ordered them to be kept at the police station temporarily for their families to claim them.

Fire at Xinzha Road

A fire broke out at 1046 Xinzha Road, Tongchang Hardware Store, yesterday morning at 2:02 AM, burning down one house. After the Fire Brigade received the news, they immediately drove to the scene to put out the fire in a short time.

Zhongda Business School Adds Chinese Shorthand Course

Taught by Master Yang Bingzhu

Since Mr. Xu Peikun took over the Zhongda Business School, there have been many improvements, and special attention has been paid to student courses. The school understands that Chinese shorthand is closely related to business students. This semester, it was decided to add a Chinese shorthand course to give students the opportunity to learn this new skill. Mr. Yang Bingxun, the inventor of the National Phonetic Shorthand, has been hired as a professor. It is said that in Shanghai, in addition to the Zhongda Business School, the College of Law and Politics, Soochow University, Fudan University, Shanghai High School, and Qingxin Middle School, etc., have also added the same course.

Air Conditioning Restored at Nanjing Grand Theatre

The air conditioner installed at the Nanjing Grand Theatre in this city stopped broadcasting cold air due to a slight breakdown of the motor some time ago. It was repaired yesterday and is back to normal operation.

Yousheng Travel Group Advanced Viewing of the Tide

The Yousheng Travel Group received a letter from its Haining members yesterday, stating that this year's tide is the largest in recent years. The group sent Zheng Jiahuan to investigate last week and confirmed that it was larger than in previous years, surging and turbulent, with some waves rising several feet above the embankment. Therefore, the group decided to advance the trip and agreed with the Railway Bureau to open a special second-class train. It will depart for Changan at 6:05 AM on the 30th of this month and return to Shanghai by the same train at 4:05 PM that afternoon. The round trip from Changhai will be handled exclusively by the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau, with a cost of six yuan (including the fare to Haining). Meals are at one's own expense. The quota is 250 people. This trip to view the tide is economical in terms of time and cost, so registrations have been very enthusiastic recently. It is said that the group is scheduled to travel to North China for half a month on the 26th of next month and will return to Shanghai at that time.

Tianyi Company to Start Filming Color Sound Film

Tianyi Film Company has recently devoted all its efforts to sound movies, hoping to win glory for the Chinese film industry. It has invested more than 400,000 yuan to purchase Movietone equipment and hired famous American photographers and sound engineers to film sound films with sound on the film. The photographer, Bert Cann, has served as the photographer for "The Moon and Sixpence" starring Fairbanks and Beanie儿, and "The Newspaper Reporter" starring Mary Brian and George O'Brien. The first sound film, "Spring Colors on the Song Stage," is about to be completed in a week. A Multicolor camera was shipped from the United States some time ago and has been installed properly. It is said that the second sound film, "Miss Shanghai," is a five-color sound film and will be started soon.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory reported at 4:30 PM yesterday that the Shanghai area was overcast with extremely strong northeasterly gusts and heavy showers. There were cyclones and rainstorms approaching the southeast of Ningbo, heading towards Hangzhou, which will cause high tides in Hangzhou Bay. There were extremely strong northeasterly to southeasterly winds in the Yellow Sea. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 83.8 and the lowest was 79.9. On the same day last year, the highest was 92.5 and the lowest was 72.9.

Letter

To the editor, yesterday I read a letter from the Shanghai County First District Office in your newspaper, which contained many concealments. On the afternoon of the 18th of this month at about 1:00 PM, our company loaded asphalt from Shanghai to the Minjing Wharf. When the porters were carrying it to the front of the store for unloading, District Chief Wu Jingqing passed by with a fierce demeanor and broke into the store. First, he smashed the abacus on the counter, and then he beat the store clerk Chen Axiao and ordered the security guards and police officers to take him to the First Public Security Bureau. He was detained for eight or nine hours, which caused public opinion to boil over and aroused public outrage. The next day, various merchants, in accordance with legal procedures, requested the Minhang Chamber of Commerce to convene a general meeting of members, and resolved to submit a request to have District Chief Wu removed from his post and investigated. The Chamber of Commerce recorded the case and reported it to the County Government. This is what happened at that time. However, the current acting chairman of the Minhang Chamber of Commerce is the accountant of the First District Office, so after the resolution of the general meeting, he tried to remedy the situation in various ways and reconvened a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees, which resolved that "a mediation should be attempted, and District Chief Wu should (A) issue a written apology, (B) compensate for the abacus and medical expenses, and (C) provide a written guarantee that he will not arbitrarily insult merchants in the future within three days." These documents are available and can be checked. In order to avoid confusion, I am writing to your newspaper to correct the record. Respectfully, Yichangxing Oil and Sesame Store, Minhang Town, August 25th, address: 55 Main Street, Minhang Town, Shanghai County.
